You can move the pointer back and forth with the < and > operators and increment and decrement the value of the cell that is actually pointed with + and -. The operator . prints the Unicode char corresponding to the value of the cell that is pointed, and the , operator assigns to the actual cell the value of the first character in the Stdin buffer.
